Having washed their hands and feet they approach the sacrificer in the ─Аgn─лdhra-chamber. The Adhvaryu rubs his hands with the formula, “May I be able (to perform the rites) for the gods through you.”1 Standing here only he gives out the call, “O Unnetr╠е, do thou place in front of the axle of the southern Havirdh─Бna cart the pressing stones, the V─Бyavya wooden cups and the Droс╣Зakala┼Ыa, putting into it the woollen fringe and filter. English

When he listens to the Hotr╠е reciting the verse, “The dawn has appeared with white cattle, fire has been laid down at the proper time; O A┼Ыvins, possessing great wealth and providing marvellous aids, your immortal chariot is yoked. O sweet ones, do you listen to my invocation,”12 (the Adhvaryu), having taken up four spoonfuls in the ladle in use, makes an offering on the ─Аhavan─лya while the sacrificer has contacted him, with the verse, тАЬMay Agni (kindled) with a fire-stick listen to my call. May the waters and the divine Dhiс╣гaс╣З─Бs listen; listen, O pressing stones, who you have known the sacrifice; may god Savitr╠е listen to my call, sv─Бh─Б."13 Having taken up another four spoonfuls and having taken up sacrificial grass, he gives out the call, “O Hotr╠е, do you summon the waters, O Camas─Бdhvaryu of Maitr─Бvaruс╣Зa, hurry up (with the goblet), O carriers of the Ekadhana pitchers, hurry up; O Neс╣гс╣нr╠е, do thou lead the sacrificer’s wife; O Unnetr╠е, do thou wait for me at the C─Бtv─Бla together with the Vasat─лvar─л water and the Hotr╠е’s goblet.”

The Neс╣гс╣нr╠е leads the sacrificer’s wife taking the p─Бnnejana vessel with the nigada-formula, “Go forth, come up towards the water which is dear to the sacrifice, may Agni lead thy head; may Aditi give thee the middle part; You are one who is released by Rudra, Yuvan by name. Do not injure me.”14 Having led her out by the eastern door, having led around along the north of the Sadas, having led around along the north of the ─Аgn─лdhr─лya mound and having gone out between the C─Бtv─Бla and the rubbish-heap, they go to the place where there is water. Having put sacrificial grass on the water, the Adhvaryu makes an offering with the formula, “O divine waters, child of the waters, do you keep with the gods that wave which serves as an oblation, mighty, most exhilerating, brilliant, for the gods drinkers of the bright (Soma) whose part you are, sv─Бh─Б.тАЭ15

English

Stooping indeed does the Adhvaryu move as the first shaking the two darbha-blades with the formula, “May the first-going speech go first. Going straight, may it go to gods, granting glory unto me, vital breath to the cattle, offspring unto me and the sacrificer.”53 They sit down in the praying place according to their seats. He gives the two darbha-blades to the Udg─Бtr╠е or the Prastotr╠е with the formula, “Thou art the spreading for R╠еk and S─Бman for the preservation by the couple,”54 or silently. Then he murmurs the introducing formula, “The him sound-maker is V─Бyu; the Prastotr╠е is Agni; the S─Бman is Praj─Бpati; the Udg─Бtr╠е is Br╠еhaspati; the Upag─Бtr╠еs are Vi┼Ыve Devas; the Pratihartr╠еs are Maruts, the ending part of S─Бman is Indra. May the gods, possessors of vital breath, give me vital breath.”55 (He further says) “Om, do you chant.”56

(With the formula) “May the wooden sword be safe; may the hammer be safe, may the rib be safe; may the altar be safe; may the axe be safe for us. The Pratiprasth─Бtr╠е pours down the remnants of his cup into the Adhvaryu’s cup. The Adhvaryu drops down half of them into the Pratiprasth─Бtr╠е’s cup.

рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕-рдкреНрд░рд╕реНрддреБрддрд┐рдГ

рддрдВ рдкреНрд░рддрд┐рдкреНрд░рд╕реНрдерд╛рддрд╛рджрд┐рддреНрдпрд╕реНрдерд╛рд▓реНрдпрд╛рдорд╡рдирдпрддрд┐ рджреЗрд╡реЗрднреНрдпрд╕реНрддреНрд╡реЗрддреНрдпрдерд╛рдзреНрд╡рд░реНрдпреБрдГ рдкреНрд░рджрдХреНрд╖рд┐рдгрдорд╛рд╡реГрддреНрдп рдкреНрд░рддреНрдпрдЩреНрдЩрд╛рджреНрд░реБрддреНрдп рд╣реЛрддреНрд░реЗ рдкрд╛рддреНрд░рдВ рдкреНрд░рджрд╛рдп рдкреНрд░рд╛рдЩрд╛рдпрдиреНрдирд╛рд╣ рдорд┐рддреНрд░рд╛рд╡рд░реБрдгрд╛рднреНрдпрд╛рдордиреБрдмреНрд░реВрд╣реАрддрд┐

рдореВрд▓рдореН

рддрдВ рдкреНрд░рддрд┐рдкреНрд░рд╕реНрдерд╛рддрд╛рджрд┐рддреНрдпрд╕реНрдерд╛рд▓реНрдпрд╛рдорд╡рдирдпрддрд┐ рджреЗрд╡реЗрднреНрдпрд╕реНрддреНрд╡реЗрддреНрдпрдерд╛рдзреНрд╡рд░реНрдпреБрдГ рдкреНрд░рджрдХреНрд╖рд┐рдгрдорд╛рд╡реГрддреНрдп рдкреНрд░рддреНрдпрдЩреНрдЩрд╛рджреНрд░реБрддреНрдп рд╣реЛрддреНрд░реЗ рдкрд╛рддреНрд░рдВ рдкреНрд░рджрд╛рдп рдкреНрд░рд╛рдЩрд╛рдпрдиреНрдирд╛рд╣ рдорд┐рддреНрд░рд╛рд╡рд░реБрдгрд╛рднреНрдпрд╛рдордиреБрдмреНрд░реВрд╣реАрддрд┐

English

The Pratiprasth─Бtr╠е pours them down in the ─Аditya vessel with the formula, “For gods thee.”75
The Adhvaryu, having turned by the right, having hastened towards the west, and having given the cup to the Hotr╠е, while going towards the east says (to the Maitr─Бvaruс╣Зa) “Do you recite the puronuv─Бky─Б for the A┼Ыvins.”

рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕-рдкреНрд░рд╕реНрддреБрддрд┐рдГ

рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕-рдкреНрд░рд╕реНрддреБрддрд┐рдГ

He causes to announce, “Do thou announce,” “Let it be heard,” “Do you address a call (to the Hotr╠е to recite the y─Бjy─Б) for the A┼Ыvins.”

At the Vaс╣гaс╣н-utterance, both of them make the offerings simultaneously. Having made the offering, he causes the sacrificer to recite the formula, “The enemy, who, O A┼Ыvins, is hostile to us, who seeks to assail us, O lords of splendour, may I here hurl him below my feet so that, O Indra, I may shine as the light.”74 The Pratiprasth─Бtr╠е pours the remnants of his cup into the Adhvaryu’s cup. The Adhvaryu pours half of both of them into the Pratiprasth─Бtr╠е’s cup.

English

They tread upon the Uttaravedi from east to west with the mantras, “In unison with Indra may we withstand our enemies, smiting the enemies irresistibly.78 O Agni, may I be brilliant with that brilliance which is thine; may I be lustrous with that lustre which is thine; may I be glowing with that glow which is thine.”78 They join the cups between the sacrificial post and the ─Аhavan─лya with the formula, “You (two) are (long) life; give me (long) life; do you give long life to the sacrifice; do you give (long) life to the lord of sacrifice. You two are the Pr─Бс╣Зa; give me Pr─Бс╣Зa; give Pr─Бс╣Зa to the sacrifice; give Pr─Бс╣Зa to the lord of sacrifice. You two are Ap─Бna; give me Ap─Бna; give Ap─Бna to the sacrifice; give Ap─Бna to the lord of sacrifice. You two are Vy─Бna; give me Vy─Бna; give Vy─Бna to the sacrifice; give Vy─Бna to the lord of sacrifice. You two are eye; give me eye; give eye to the sacrifice; give eye to the lord of sacrifice. You two are ear; give me ear; give ear to the sacrifice; give ear to the lord of sacrifice.”77

The Adhvaryu throws one with the formula, “┼Ъaс╣Зс╕Нa is thrown away with this.” He thinks of him whom the sacrificer hates.

The Pratiprasth─Бtr╠е causes to announce: “Do thou announce;” “May it be heard;тАЭ тАЬO reciter of the ┼Ъastra, do you recite the y─Бjy─Б (for the offering) of the Somas.”

English

He offers twice at the Vaс╣гaс╣н and the second Vaс╣гaс╣н-utterance. Similarly (the Camas─Бdhvaryus) offer all the goblets twice.
Having turned by the right, (the Pratiprasth─Бtr╠е) pours down the remnants in Acch─Бv─Бka’s goblet with the formula, “I pour thee the offered into the offered, granting vigour to the gods and yielding into the offered, granting vigour to the gods and yielding honey for men” or silently. Having kept down the cup there only, they move towards the west together with the consumable Somas. The Savanabhakс╣гa formula following (the invocation of Iс╕Н─Б) is “…drunk by Indra-Agni….” The three (namely, the Acch─Бv─Бka, the Adhvaryu and the Pratiprasth─Бtr╠е) consume Acch─Бv─Бka’s goblet, after having obtained the consent of each other.
